Many folks also cut into the line from across the street. This should be deemed unsafe as pedestrians should be lined up to the left sidewalk nearby where the free food event is being held.

<Gmap_id>0x80857e11b4f9c7f1:0x33e9b83728db8ccf</Gmap_id>< Text>
Great organization. Clearly serving people in need. Staff and volunteers are warm and welcoming. Flexible about what they will accept (e.g., they take kids' clothing). They give away donated goods rather than sell them like the huge corporate thrift stores. This is a grassroots organization that serves the community in which it is located. It's my favorite place to donate clothing and household goods. Highly recommended!</Text>

< Text>
I went back a two days after my first visit...great tacos!! The prices are fantastic and the tacos are stuffed.

My order was quick coming out and the staff were friendly and helpful. Good vegan & gf options (hongos tacos!).

Sitting upstairs offers a great view of Telegraph, but if it's a hot day be prepared to be a little hotter up there. The back patio seating is chill and a great place to sit and talk.

Definitely recommend!<//Text>

< Review>
Or at least it feels like it does. It's chicken soup with grilled chicken, tortilla strips, a little bit of heat and a lot of lime, and even with a cold you can taste it, and feel it working. My friend got the Danger Dog, a bacon-wrapped hot dog in a flour tortilla with all the fixings and she was loving it. The brownie was moist and big enough to split (full disclosure -- I couldn't taste it because of my cold, but my friend said it was delish). Ordering at the counter is quick and the food comes out fast and delicious, so don't mind the line, you'll get to where you're going in time. It's one of the cheaper alternatives before a concert at the Fox or the Paramount. There's table seating on the main floor, upstairs, and a small patio outside in the back. A large-screen tv downstairs shows mostly local sports or soccer.</Review>

< Text>
Went with my wife. Enjoyed some very nice Horchata while devouring 3 tacos each. They were a tad greasy because this place loves melted cheese. They are also small, as others have mentioned. However, they are much wider than most, and I still found myself full.

Their cabbage + lime + cilantro topping is superb, and a dash of their table-top hot sauce topped it off.

Overall, it was very nice. The atmosphere was nice and quiet on a Saturday night. The staff was very friendly and helpful. It felt very clean as well.</Text>

<UserId.>102025853531471968865< /UserId.><gmap_id>0x808f80b274a0f49b:0x1e1821f195ca9615<//gmap_id><Date>1555389859857< /Date><resp>None< /resp>< user_name>
E B< /user_name>
< Review>
I got the NOPALES burrito and it was AMAZING! it had a spicy pumpkin seed based sauce and eggs and potatoes and delicious black refried beans and so much deliciousness. I thought it had chorizo but I was wrong and frankly, I didn't miss it at all. Would definitely order it again and recommend everyone try it at least once because it clearly has some very Mexican flavors that you don't usually get at burrito places.

Edit: I went back! It was in the afternoon so they didn't have the burrito anymore as it's only for breakfast. I'm hooked on the nopales so I got a tostada with them and also their "Lima soup" which is a super deliciously tangy limey chicken tortilla strip soup. The chicken in the soup was a little overcooked but the broth was so good I didn't mind, that broth is the broth of my dreams. The other thing could be fixed is that the chips were cold but OMG their guacamole was perfection! Highly recommend for their vegetarian/vegan options and for people who want to try some authentic Mexican cactus YUM<//Review>

<text>Xolo is my go-to place when I head to a show at the Fox. It's across the street, has delish food, is relatively inexpensive, and they are fast! My fave order consists of the Vampiro and Machaca tacos. The Vapiro taco is a cheesy corn tortilla filled with perfectly seasoned al pastor crisped to perfection. The Machaca taco is also a corn tortilla but it is stuffed with tender, juicy, slow cooked beef that is shredded and accompanied by soft, sweet bell peppers and onions.
